text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Every month i allow my\ncrew to meditate via the back door.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is important for\ntheir mental health, in a chemical field fraught with danger.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The motto on board is\nWORK HARD PLAY HARD.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Every day we play with\ndeadly chemicals on our stainless steel chemical tanker.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Mind you, this field is\nmerciless and unforgiving. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It saps your will, if\nyou cant win against the elements hurled against you day after day , hour after\nhour--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The work is enervating.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">My wife , who has\nsailed with me for 9 years , sometimes asks me -- why don't you retire from\nchemicals tankers and do something more safer. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">This will be like\nasking a tiger who tastes blood daily to eat grass, or a shark which needs the\ndeep ocean salt water ( read as pressure ) to flow past its gills , to swim in\na mangy chlorinated swimming pool..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\"Meditation via\nback door concept \" was first propounded by OSHO, a very intelligent man--\n.&nbsp; He had the answers to life management.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">YOU MAKE YOURSELF DOG\nTIRED IN A MEDIUM YOU LOVE --&nbsp; IT COULD\nBE DANCING --&nbsp; AFTER THAT GO TO SLEEP.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After the storm comes\nthe peace ( maan, don't ask me how many pieces ) .<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;\">\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Piece -- nay-- peace ,\ncomes to you whether you like it or not.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UHtpZE9U6Nw/TjGNyMoaXII/AAAAAAAAEsc/63BptIyOCQo/s1600/magda+1.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UHtpZE9U6Nw/TjGNyMoaXII/AAAAAAAAEsc/63BptIyOCQo/s640/magda+1.JPG\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I assure my crew\ncontinuous rest of 12 hours after such a \" meditation \" session. At\nsea we don't have the pleasure of shoving peace down our throats, by proper\ntime consuming meditation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When they wake up they\nfeel like babies.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I tell my officers to\nkeep their stripes and attitudes in their cabins , before they come down to the\nlounge for the party. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">No coming to the party\nwith old baggage.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">For they have to jump\ninto the melting pot. They have to place their ego on the back burner or rather\nmelt their egos, and gel with their subordinates, once a month.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I keep a hawk's eye --\nyet nobody knows this, or cares --.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">For if a leader cant\nbond with his team in harmony in times of peace , how can he bond with them\nwhen shit hits the fan--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">-- in the midst of a\nraging fire and bodies and limbs strewn around you, after an explosion?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">In the party all are\nequal.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">There is nobody more\nequal than the other. I have NOT yet seen anybody taking advantage of this\nrelaxation of discipline.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Watch the video once\nmore--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">-- it is the equivalent\nof Manmohan Singh ( Chief Engineer ) and Prathibha Patil ( I the Captain )\ndancing with the entire Lok Sabha ( deck crew ) and Rajya Sabha ( engine crew )\n.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is NOT about dancing\nentirely--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both;\">\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">-- we have fun--&nbsp; we talk -- we converse-- we sing-- we crack\njokes - we reminisce--<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"background-color: yellow; color: blue; font-size: large;\"><b>No one-up-manship -- no putting people in their places --&nbsp; no chattering minds --&nbsp; no self delusions -- no hidden agendas--&nbsp; no over inflated self importance --&nbsp; no distorted interpretations -- no selective perceptions --&nbsp; no staring into the rear view mirror --&nbsp; no self pity -- no resentments-- </b></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FxaOn8KjDqI/TjAZ4wQmlII/AAAAAAAAEoY/Lux8SW8vVNk/s1600/work+hard+play+hard+fcol.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"345\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-FxaOn8KjDqI/TjAZ4wQmlII/AAAAAAAAEoY/Lux8SW8vVNk/s640/work+hard+play+hard+fcol.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nyes-- you may call this Utopia--&nbsp; all are in the moment--</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">No placing one leg in the past and one in the future , to piss on the present--</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nThis does NOT mean next day my steward will try and be familiar with me-- and pat my back and say \" hi buddy!\".&nbsp;&nbsp; Rather he will be grateful, that I have treated him like a brother and friend -- nay-- human being ,&nbsp; for 4 hours in a month.</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nMy crew knows that captain does NOT like sick poultry -- that he rarely punishes a man who will be the life of&nbsp;a party -- who is a good shipmate --</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nthis encourages them to let their hair down --</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\nand</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"color: red;\">RELEASE THEIR LOCKED UP STRESSES </span>!</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; important scavenge drains . it deserves an check/ overhaul <br />\nevery month. <br />\n<br />\n-- and then the scavenge air receiver and the underpiston space become <br />\nswimming pools--from where water will be churned into the cylinders <br />\nwith every blast before and after BDC via scavenge ports.<br />\n<br />\nTHIS WILL SHATTER THE PISTON RINGS.<br />\n<br />\nin such a case it pays to increase the scav air temp to 48 deg c ( not <br />\nmore ).<br />\n<br />\nXXX should not worry about sulphurous acid-- this can come only if <br />\nthe sulphur content is high. <br />\n<br />\nour santos bunkers have 0.5% sulphur. in any case this acid serves to<br />\n&nbsp;clean the keechad from liner honed grooves, which act as reservoirs<br />\n&nbsp;for the mecyl..<br />\n<br />\nas of today now we need to clean our aircooler ( 52 deg c ) - anything <br />\nmore than 48 deg c and the main engine loses power.<br />\n<br />\nin the april XXX meet 2nd engr XXX said that \" the ME air cooler <br />\ncovers are holed \" .&nbsp;
